APPENDIX C. GOLD ETCHANT APV
Design, Fabrication and Characterization of a CMUT for a Linear Array Probe
131
==PAGE:140==
 
The template is filled out based on knowledge of the work processes and relevant chemical instructions 
in Kemibrug.dk 
 
DETAILS OF THE WORK PROCESS 
Details can be presented as a flow diagram of the process – i.e. broken down into logical sub-processes. 
The Transene GE-8110 is only used or prepared in a fume hood and while wearing safety glasses, 4H 
barrier gloves and 4H barrier apron. 
 
1. The etchant is poured into a glass beaker. The amount will vary depending on the amount of 
wafers and the wafer holder used (≈600 mL for a horizontal holder and 1.2 L for a vertical holder) 
2. Wafers are fixed in a vertical or horizontal wafer holder 
3. Holder is placed in beaker and is etched for the designated etching time. 
4. Wafers are transferred to a quick dump rinse bath in the fume hood for 5 minutes with spraying. Repeat 
if there are residues until there is no traces left. 
5. Remaining Transene GE-8110 is poured back into the bottle using a funnel.

APPENDIX C. GOLD ETCHANT APV
Design, Fabrication and Characterization of a CMUT for a Linear Array Probe
133
==PAGE:142==
 
The template is filled out based on knowledge of the work processes and relevant chemical instructions 
in Kemibrug.dk 
HAZARDS FROM THE WORK PROCESS 
What risks can be foreseen in relation to: 
- Handling (e.g. mixing of reactive chemicals, pressure, vacuum, temperature, fire hazard) 
Chance of spilling when pouring, but colour of liquid makes it easy to see any drops spilled. 
 
- The working processes (e.g. glass equipment under vacuum with risk of blasting) 
 
- Equipment (e.g. power failure in relation to the function of the equipment and nature of the work) 
 
- Storage of purchased and manufactured chemicals (e.g. risk of peroxide formation, test semi-annually) 
Store in a ventilated cupboard at temperatures below 27 °C 
- Transport (e.g. Waste when transporting chemicals from A to B) 
Use a chemical transport trolley when transporting. Only closed beakers are allowed to be transported. 
 
RISK OF EXPOSURE AND PRECAUTIONS 
Assess the real risk of exposure in all sub-processes. (The fact that the chemicals are dangerous by inhalation 
does not mean that there is a risk of inhalation in this work process). 
What precautions should be taken to prevent / minimize risks and exposure? (Encapsulation, Extraction, Closed 
systems, Personal protective equipment, Remove static electricity / Sparks / Heat / Oxygen concentration, 
Pressure, Temperature, Inert conditions, Quantity, Concentration, Transport, Equipment control, Other persons 
Access to the room, Limit the number of people to be exposed or limit the duration of time of exposure) 
4H gloves and safety glasses are worn at all times (Face shield can be used instead of safety glasses). 
When handling/pouring the chemical and during cleaning a 4H barrier apron must be worn. 
Must only be opened inside a fume hood. 
 
SUBSTITUTION 
Describe what attempts and considerations have been made in relation to substitution of hazardous chemicals or 
work processes. (Remember, that reduced quantities instead of large ones, is also substitution). 
An unbuffered version Transene GE-8111 exists, and a faster etching Transene GE-8148 is available. 
They are all Iodine based as well and Transene GE-8110 is chosen for the lower etch rate and it being 
buffered.

WHAT TO DO IN THE EVENT OF AN ACCIDENT OR SPILLAGE?? 
Describe the action and safety precautions for relevant accidents, for example: 
- Exposure to the chemical (emergency equipment, first aid, Kemibrug safety data sheets are brought to the 
emergency room) and any subsequent occupational medical examinations 
- Chemical spillage (safe collection and disposal of waste, which waste kit must be within reach, which personal 
protective equipment must be available, consider the evacuation) 
- Other (e.g. fire, gas alarm, power failure) (e.g. safe stop of experiments, block up the area, press the fire alarm 
or other alarms, evacuation, safe removal of organic liquids and pressure bottles, close equipment’s) 
- If external help is called: Local emergency instructions and contact with DTU corporate emergency team  
 
Prevent further spreading and ventilate the area. 
Avoid contact with the substance. If appropriate, use gloves and breathing equipment with a 
combination filter (Type ABEK-P). 
Soak up any spillages with vermiculite or sand and discard as chemical waste 
Clean the area after clearing up the spillage. 
Inform the municipal authorities and those responsible for the environment in the workplace of any 
major discharge into the surroundings.
